<p class=MsoNormal>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Answer:
<u>blastopore<o:p></o:p></u></p>

<p class=MsoNormal>One of the two distinct branches of coelomates, consisting
of the annelids, mollusks, and arthropods, and characterized by spiral,
determinate cleavage, schizocoelous formation of the coelom, and development of
the mouth from the blastopore.</p>

<p class=MsoNormal>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Answer:
<u>protostomes</u></p>

<p class=MsoNormal>The other branch of coelemates, consisting of the
echinoderms and chordates and characterized by radial, indeterminate cleavage,
enterocoelous formation of the coelom, and development of the anus from the
blastopore.</p>

<p class=MsoNormal>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Answer:
<u>deuterostomes</u></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></p>

<p class=MsoNormal>120) Identify the following terms related to sponges from
their definitions for five points each.</p>

<p class=MsoNormal>The central cavity of a sponge.</p>

<p class=MsoNormal>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Answer:
<u>spongocoel</u></p>

<p class=MsoNormal>The opening of the spongocoel.</p>

<p class=MsoNormal>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Answer:
<u>osculum</u></p>

<p class=MsoNormal>A gelatinous region separating the two layers of cells in a
sponge.</p>

<p class=MsoNormal>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Answer:
<u>mesohyl</u></p>

<p class=MsoNormal>Cells which trap food.</p>

<p class=MsoNormal>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Answer:
<u>choanocytes</u></p>

<p class=MsoNormal>Cells which take up food and carry nutrients to other <span
class=GramE>cells, and</span> have pseudopodia.</p>

<p class=MsoNormal>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Answer:
<u>amoebocytes<o:p></o:p></u></p>

<p class=MsoNormal>An individual which functions as both male and female,
producing eggs and sperm.</p>

<p class=MsoNormal>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Answer:
<u>hermaphrodite</u></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></p>

<p class=MsoNormal>121) Identify the following terms related to cnidarians from
their definitions for five points each.</p>

<p class=MsoNormal>The central digestive compartment of a cnidarian.</p>

<p class=MsoNormal>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Answer:
<u>gastrovascular cavity</u></p>

<p class=MsoNormal>The sessile cylindrical variant form of the cniderian body
plan, which adheres to a substratum by the aboral end and extends its
tentacles, waiting for prey. Examples of cnidarians with this body plan include
hydras and sea anemones.</p>

<p class=MsoNormal>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Answer:
<u>polyps</u></p>

<p class=MsoNormal>The floating, flattened, mouth-down variant form of the
cniderian body plan, which moves freely in the water. Examples of cnidarians
with this body plan include jellyfish.</p>

<p class=MsoNormal>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Answer:
<u>medusas</u></p>

<p class=MsoNormal>Unique cells on cnidarian tentacles that function in defense
and the capture of prey.</p>

<p class=MsoNormal>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Answer:
<u>cnidocytes</u></p>

<p class=MsoNormal>Organelles in cnidocytes capable of everting.</p>

<p class=MsoNormal>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Answer:
<u>cnidae</u></p>

<p class=MsoNormal>Cnidae which can sting.</p>

<p class=MsoNormal>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Answer:
<u>nematocysts</u></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></p>

<p class=MsoNormal>122) Answer the following related to mollusks for six points
each.</p>

<p class=MsoNormal>The body of a mollusk has three main parts. One is a
muscular organ used for movement, another is the region which contains most of
the internal organs, and the third is a fold of tissue that drapes over this
region and secretes a shell. Name these three parts, respectively.</p>

<p class=MsoNormal>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Answer:

<u>trochophore</u></p>

<p class=MsoNormal>123) Identify the following terms related to arthropods from

<p class=MsoNormal>An exoskeleton constructed from layers of protein and chitin
which completely covers the body of an arthropod.</p>

<p class=MsoNormal>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Answer:

<p class=MsoNormal>The process of shedding an exoskeleton and secreting a

<p class=MsoNormal>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Answer:

<p class=MsoNormal>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Answer:

<p class=MsoNormal>An organ in most spiders consisting of stacked plates in an

<u>book lungs</u> (prompt on lungs)</p>

<p class=MsoNormal>Unique excretory organs in insects that empty into the

<p class=MsoNormal>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Answer:
<u>Malpighian tubules</u></p>

<p class=MsoNormal>124) Identify the following terms related to egg production
